<script>
    var loc_main = "https://www.dial4trade.com";

    $(document).on('keypress', '#mobile', function() {
        $('#mob_err').hide();
        var attrbb = $(this).closest('.intl-tel-input').find('#getCntryFrm');
        var contcd = $(this).closest('.intl-tel-input').find('.iti-flag');
        var cntclass = contcd.attr('class');
        var splclass = cntclass.split(" ");
        var cntcd = splclass[1].toUpperCase()

        $('#contcode').val(cntcd);
        var gettitleval = attrbb.attr('title');
        if (gettitleval != $('#ph_ccode').val()) {
            $('#ph_ccode').val(gettitleval);
            $('#mobile').val('');
        }
        var mobile_number = $("#mobile").val();

        if (gettitleval == "91") {
            if (String(mobile_number).charAt(0) < 6 && mobile_number.length > 1) {
                $('#mob_err').show();
                $('#mobile').addClass('error_bdr');
                document.getElementById('mobile').focus();
                return false;
            } else {
                $('#mob_err').hide();
            }
        }
    });
    $(document).on('click', '#mobile', function() {

        $('#mob_err').hide();
        var attrbb = $(this).closest('.intl-tel-input').find('#getCntryFrm');
        var gettitleval = attrbb.attr('title');

        if (gettitleval != $('#ph_ccode').val()) {
            $('#ph_ccode').val(gettitleval);
            $('#mobile').val('');
        }
        var mobile_number = $("#mobile").val();

        if (gettitleval == "91") {
            $('#mobile').attr('minlength', '10');
            $('#mobile').attr('maxlength', '10');

            if (String(mobile_number).charAt(0) < 6 && mobile_number.length > 1) {
                $('#mob_err').show();
                $('#mobile').addClass('error_bdr');

                document.getElementById('pqmobile').focus();
                return false;
            } else {
                $('#mob_err').hide();
            }
        } else {
            $('#mobile').attr('minlength', '5');
            $('#mobile').attr('maxlength', '15');

            var attrbb = $(this).closest('.intl-tel-input').find('#getCntryFrm');
            var gettitleval = attrbb.attr('title');
            $('#ph_ccode').val(gettitleval);
        }
    });
    $(document).ready(function() {
        $("#city").keyup(function() {
            $("#popup_req_city_suggestion").hide();

            if ($(this).val().length < 3) {
                $("#popup_req_city_suggestion").hide();
                return;
            }

            if ($("#ph_ccode").val() != '91' && $("#ph_ccode").val() != '') {
                $("#popup_req_city_suggestion").hide();
                return;
            }
            $.ajax({
                type: "POST",
                url: loc_main + "/ajax323/suggetions_list.php",
                data: 'action_id=city&letters=' + $(this).val(),
                beforeSend: function() {
                    $("#city").css("background", "#FFF url() no-repeat 165px");
                },
                success: function(data) {
                    $("#popup_req_city_suggestion").show();
                    $("#popup_req_city_suggestion").html(data);
                    $("#city").css("background", "#FFF");
                }
            });
        });
    });

    jQuery.validator.addMethod("emailordomain", function(value, element) {
        return this.optional(element) || /^\w+@[a-zA-Z_]+?\.[a-zA-Z]{2,3}$/.test(value) || /[-a-zA-Z0-9@:%_\+.~#?&//=]{2,256}\.[a-z]{2,20}\b(\/[-a-zA-Z0-9@:%_\+.~#?&//=]*)?/.test(value);
    }, "");


    $("#post_req_form").validate({
        rules: {
            subject: {required: true,  minlength: 3  },
            quantityNo: {
                required: function(element) {
                    if ($("#quantityType").val().length > 0) {
                        return true;
                    } else {
                        return false;
                    }
                }
            },
            quantityType: {
                required: function(element) {
                    if ($("#quantityNo").val().length > 0) {
                        return true;
                    } else {
                        return false;
                    }
                }
            },
            your_name: {
                required: true,
                minlength: 3,
                maxlength: 30
            },
            email: {
                required: true,
                emailordomain: true,
                email: true,
            },
            mobile: {
                required: true,
                minlength: function(element) {
                    if ($("#ph_ccode").val() == '91') {
                        return 10;
                    } else {
                        return 5;
                    }
                },
                maxlength: function(element) {
                    if ($("#ph_ccode").val() == '91') {
                        return 10;
                    } else {
                        return 15;
                    }
                }
            },
            city: {
                required: true
            },
        },
        messages: {
            subject: {
                required: "",
                minlength: ""
            },
            quantityNo: "",
            quantityType: "",
            your_name: {
                required: "",
                minlength: "",
                maxlength: ""
            },
            email: {
                required: "",
                email: ""
            },
            mobile: {
                required: "",
                minlength: ""
            },
            city: ""
        },
        highlight: function(element) {
            $(element).addClass('error_bdr');
        },
        unhighlight: function(element) {
            $(element).removeClass('error_bdr');
        },
        submitHandler: function(form) {

            var subject = $('#subject').val();
            var detail_req = $('#detail_req').val();
            var your_name = $('#your_name').val();
            var email = $('#email').val();

            var city = $('#city').val();
            var quantityNo = $('#quantityNo').val();
            var quantityType = $('#finalQuantityType').val();
            var ph_ccode = $('#ph_ccode').val();
            var comp_name = $('#comp_name').val();
            var source = $('#source').val();
            var contcode = $('#contcode').val();
             var city_hidden = $('#pqcity_hidden').val();
             var product_id  = $('#product_id').val();
             var whatsappno1 = $('#whatsappno1').prop('checked') ? 1 : 0;
              var checkIcon = ` <svg width="12" height="11" viewBox="0 0 16 11" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M1 5.4L5.4 9.8L14.2 1" stroke="white" stroke-width="1.76" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"></path> </svg>`;
            $.ajax({
                type: 'POST',
                url: 'https://www.dial4trade.com/popup_inquiry_v7.php',
                // data: 'frm=popup&action_enquiry=popInquiryFrm&inqfrm=sendInq&prod_name=' + subject + '&prod_desc=' + detail_req + '&mem_name=' + your_name + '&mem_email=' + email + '&mobile=' + mobile + '&city=' + city + '&prod_qnty=' + quantityNo + '&qnty_type=' + quantityType + '&OrderUnitInput=&mem_compname=' + comp_name + '&city_hidden=' + city_hidden + '&product_id=' + product_id + '&ph_ccode=' + ph_ccode + '&cont_ccode=' + contcode + '&popCompSrc=' + source,
                data:'frm=popup' +'&action_enquiry=popInquiryFrm' +'&inqfrm=sendInq' +'&prod_name=' + encodeURIComponent(subject) +'&prod_desc=' + encodeURIComponent(detail_req) +'&mem_name=' + encodeURIComponent(your_name) +'&mem_email=' + encodeURIComponent(email) +'&mobile=' + encodeURIComponent(mobile) +'&city=' + encodeURIComponent(city) +'&prod_qnty=' + encodeURIComponent(quantityNo) +'&qnty_type=' + encodeURIComponent(quantityType) +'&OrderUnitInput=' +'&mem_compname=' + encodeURIComponent(comp_name) +'&city_hidden=' + encodeURIComponent(city_hidden) +'&product_id=' + encodeURIComponent(product_id) +'&ph_ccode=' + encodeURIComponent(ph_ccode) +'&cont_ccode=' + encodeURIComponent(contcode) +'&popCompSrc=' + encodeURIComponent(source) +'&whatsappno2=' + whatsappno1,
                success: function(msg) {

                        .html(checkIcon);
                    if (msg == 'done') {
                        $('#post-buy-req-modal').hide();
                        $("#inqstep-1").html('');
                        $("#companyInquiry").hide();
                        $("#modal2-thanks").show();
                    }

                    var msg = msg.replace(/\s/g, "");
                    var msgval = msg.split("^");

                    if (msgval[0] == 'blockmem') {
                        $("#btninquiry").html('Your account is locked, due suspicious activity is detected.');
                        $("#mbtmsubmit").html('Your account is locked, due suspicious activity is detected.');

                                $('#compLogDis').html('')
                                $('#companyInquiry').show();
                                $("#inqstep-1").html('');
                                $("#inqstep-1").html(msg1);
                            }
                        });
                    }

                    if (msgval[0] == 'send_otp_email') {

                                    );
                                    $('#compDePopDisp').hide();
                                    $('#cont_comp_nameV').html('<ul class="mb2_prd_dtail mt-3 mb-3"><li class="title">How it Works</li></ul>	<ul class="modal-hiw"><li>Tell us what you need by filling the form</li>                                <li>Receive Verified supplier details</li>                                <li>Compare Quotations and seal the deal</li>                            </ul>');
                                    $('#compLogDis').html('');
                                    $('#companyInquiry').show();
                                    $("#inqstep-1").html('');
                                    $("#inqstep-1").html(msg1);
                                }
                            }
                        });
                    }
                }
            });

        }
    });

    function isNumberKey(evt) {
        var charCode = (evt.which) ? evt.which : event.keyCode;
        if (charCode != 46) {
            if (charCode > 31 && (charCode < 48 || charCode > 57)) {
                return false;
            } else {
                return true;
            }
        }
    }
    $(document).ready(function() {

        var $scope = $('#order-unit-form');
        if (!$scope.length) return;

        // Select change
        $scope.on('change', '.OrderUnitSelect', function() {
            var val = $(this).val();

            if (val === 'other') {
                $scope.find('.OrderUnitInput-wrap').show();
                $scope.find('.OrderUnitInput').val('');
                $scope.find('#finalQuantityType').val('');
            } else {
                $scope.find('.OrderUnitInput-wrap').hide();
                $scope.find('.OrderUnitInput').val('');
                $scope.find('#finalQuantityType').val(val);
            }
        });

        // Typing in "Other"
        $scope.on('keyup', '.OrderUnitInput', function(e) {
            e.stopPropagation();

            var value = $(this).val().trim();
            $scope.find('#finalQuantityType').val(value);

            var $list = $scope.find('.unit-list');
            $list.find('li').hide();

            if (value !== '') {
                $list.find('span:contains("' + value + '")')
                    .closest('li')
                    .show();
                $list.show();
            }
        });

        // Case-insensitive contains
        $.expr[":"].contains = $.expr.createPseudo(function(arg) {
            return function(elem) {
                return $(elem).text().toUpperCase().indexOf(arg.toUpperCase()) >= 0;
            };
        });

        // Click suggestion
        $scope.on('click', '.unit-list span', function(e) {
            e.stopPropagation();
            var unitValue = $(this).text();

            $scope.find('.OrderUnitInput').val(unitValue);
            $scope.find('#finalQuantityType').val(unitValue);
            $scope.find('.unit-list').hide();
        });

        // Show suggestions on input focus
        $scope.on('focus', '.OrderUnitInput', function(e) {
            e.stopPropagation();
            $scope.find('.unit-list').show();
        });

        // Hide on body click (only this scope)
        $(document).on('click', function() {
            $scope.find('.unit-list').hide();
        });

    });
    $(document).on('keypress', '#mobile', function() {
        $('#mob_err').hide();
        var attrbb = $(this).closest('.intl-tel-input').find('#getCntryFrm');
        var contcd = $(this).closest('.intl-tel-input').find('.iti-flag');
        var cntclass = contcd.attr('class');
        var splclass = cntclass.split(" ");
        var cntcd = splclass[1].toUpperCase()

        $('#contcode').val(cntcd);
        var gettitleval = attrbb.attr('title');
        if (gettitleval != $('#ph_ccode').val()) {
            $('#ph_ccode').val(gettitleval);
            $('#mobile').val('');
        }
        var mobile_number = $("#mobile").val();

        if (gettitleval == "91") {
            if (String(mobile_number).charAt(0) < 6 && mobile_number.length > 1) {
                $('#mob_err').show();
                $('#mobile').addClass('error_bdr');
                document.getElementById('mobile').focus();
                return false;
            } else {
                $('#mob_err').hide();
            }
        }
    });
    function allLetterreq(evt) {

        var charCode = (evt.which) ? evt.which : event.keyCode;
        if (charCode != 46 && charCode != 32) {
            if (charCode > 31 && ((charCode > 64 && charCode < 91) || (charCode > 96 && charCode < 123))) {
                return true;
            } else {
                return false;
            }
        }
    }

    function readCookieclass(name) {
        var nameEQ = name + "=";
        var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
        for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
            var c = ca[i];
            while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') c = c.substring(1, c.length);
            if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length, c.length);
        }
        return null;
    }

    $(document).ready(function() {

        var memberName = readCookieclass('memberName');
        var email = readCookieclass('email');
        var mobileNo = readCookieclass('mobileNo');
        var sessionID = readCookieclass('sessionID');
        var city = readCookieclass('city');
        var countryCodePhone = readCookieclass('countryCodePhone');
        var country = readCookieclass('country');
        var companyName = readCookieclass('companyName');
        var countryCode = readCookieclass('countryCode');
        var verified_contact = readCookieclass('verified_contact');

        var avail_on_whatsapp = readCookieclass("avail_on_whatsapp");
        if (sessionID != '' && sessionID != null) {

if (avail_on_whatsapp == "1") {

    $("#whatsappno1, #whatsappno2, #whatsappno3")
        .prop("checked", true)
        .prop("disabled", true);
        $(".whatsapp-label").addClass("disabled-whatsapp").css("pointer-events", "none");
        $(".whatsnumb").find("#whatsappno3").prop("checked", true)
        .prop("disabled", true);
}
            if (memberName != '' && memberName != null) {
                var resmemberName = decodeURIComponent(memberName.replace(/\+/g, ' '));
                $('#your_name').val(resmemberName);
            }
            if (email != '' && email != null) {
                var res = decodeURIComponent(email.replace(/\+/g, ' '));
                $('#email').val(res);
                   if(verified_contact == 'V'){
                $('#email').attr('readonly', true);
                    $('#email').attr('disabled', true);
            }
            }
            if (mobileNo != '' && mobileNo != null) {
                $('#mobile').val(mobileNo);
                
            }
            if (countryCodePhone != '' && countryCodePhone != null) {
                $('#ph_ccode').val(countryCodePhone);
                if(verified_contact == 'V'){
                    $('#mobile').attr('readonly', true);
                    $('#mobile').attr('disabled', true);
                     // Disable flag dropdown
                    $('.selected-flag').addClass('disabled-flag');
                    $('.selected-flag').css({
                        'pointer-events': 'none',
                        'opacity': '0.6'
                    });
                }
                $('#getCntryFrm').attr('title', countryCodePhone);

                if (countryCode != '' && countryCode != null) {
                	$('#getCntryFrm').closest('.iti-flag').find('.iti-flag').removeClass('in');
                	$('#getCntryFrm').closest('.iti-flag').find('.iti-flag').addClass(countryCode);
                } else if (countryCodePhone == '91') {
                	$('#getCntryFrm').closest('.iti-flag').find('.iti-flag').addClass('in');
                }

            }


            if (countryCode != '' && countryCode != null) {
                $('#contcode').val(countryCode);
                $('.selected-flag .iti-flag').removeClass('in');
                $('.selected-flag .iti-flag').addClass(countryCode);
            } else {
                var $activeCountry = $('.appendCountryList .country-list .country.active');
               
                console.log('Country Code Phone 1:', countryCodePhone);
                if ($activeCountry.length && countryCodePhone != '' && countryCodePhone != null) {
                     console.log('Country Code Phone 2:', countryCodePhone);
                    if (countryCodePhone == '91') {
                        $('.selected-flag .iti-flag').removeClass('in');
                    }
                    var cc_code = $('#country_code_flag').val();

                    // Get ISO class from flag
                    var flagClass = $activeCountry.find('.iti-flag').attr('class');
                    var iso = flagClass.replace('iti-flag', '').trim(); // => "jp"

                    // Apply to selected flag container
                    var $targetFlag = $('#post_req_form').find('.selected-flag').find('.iti-flag');

                    // Reset & apply
                    $targetFlag.attr('class', 'iti-flag ' + cc_code);
                    $('#post_req_form').find('.selected-flag').attr('dial-code', countryCodePhone);
                    $('#post_req_form').find('.selected-flag').attr('title', countryCodePhone);
                    $('#post_req_form').find('#contcode').val(cc_code);
                    $('#ph_ccode').val(countryCodePhone);
                     $('.selected-flag .iti-flag').addClass(iso);
                }
            }
            if (city != '' && city != null) {
                var rescity = decodeURIComponent(city.replace(/\+/g, ' '));
                $('#city').val(rescity);
            }
            if (sessionID != '' && sessionID != null) {
                var sstr = sessionID
                var sres = sstr.split("%7E");
                //$('#memberID').val(sres[0]);
            }
            if (companyName != '' && companyName != null) {
                var compname = decodeURIComponent(companyName.replace(/\+/g, ' '))
                $('#comp_name').val(compname);
            }
        }

        
    });

var loc_main = "https://www.dial4trade.com";

function allLetterreq(evt) {
	
	var charCode = (evt.which) ? evt.which : event.keyCode;
	if (charCode != 46 && charCode != 32) {
		if (charCode > 31 && ((charCode > 64 && charCode < 91) || (charCode > 96 && charCode < 123))) {
			return true;
		}
		else {
			return false;
		}
	}
}

function isNumberKey(evt) {
	var charCode = (evt.which) ? evt.which : event.keyCode;
	if (charCode!=46) {if (charCode > 31 && (charCode < 48 || charCode > 57)) {return false;}else {return true;}}
}


function readCookieclass(name) {
	var nameEQ = name + "=";
	var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
	for(var i=0;i < ca.length;i++) {
		var c = ca[i];
		while (c.charAt(0)==' ') c = c.substring(1,c.length);
		if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length,c.length);
	}
	return null;
}

<script>
	
	function allLetterreq(evt) {
	
	var charCode = (evt.which) ? evt.which : event.keyCode;
	if (charCode != 46 && charCode != 32) {
		if (charCode > 31 && ((charCode > 64 && charCode < 91) || (charCode > 96 && charCode < 123))) {
			return true;
		}
		else {
			return false;
		}
	}
}


window.onload = function() {
    var xhr = new XMLHttpRequest();
    xhr.open('GET', 'https://www.dial4trade.com/index-login.php', true);
    xhr.onreadystatechange = function() {
        if (xhr.readyState === 4 && xhr.status === 200) {
			if(xhr.responseText!='') {
				$('#logind').html(xhr.responseText);
				$('#trenProd').html('');
			}
        }
    };
    xhr.send();
	
	
	var xhr1 = new XMLHttpRequest();
    xhr1.open('GET', 'https://www.dial4trade.com/index-banner.php', true);
    xhr1.onreadystatechange = function() {
        if (xhr1.readyState === 4 && xhr1.status === 200) {
			if(xhr1.responseText!='') {
				$('#dipHBan').html(xhr1.responseText);
			}
        }
    };
    xhr1.send();
	
};

</script>

<script>
$(document).on('click', '#downloadmobile', function(){
	
	var attrbb = $(this).closest('.intl-tel-input').find('#getCntryFrm');
	var gettitleval=attrbb.attr('title');
	
	$('#dmpqph_ccode').val(gettitleval);
	
	if(gettitleval=="91" && gettitleval!=null) {
		$('#downloademail').hide();
		$('#dispvalsme').html('mobile number');
		$('#sndtxt').html('Text me the link');
		
	}
	else {
		$('#downloademail').show();
		$('#dispvalsme').html('email id');
		$('#sndtxt').html('Send me the link');
	}
});


$(document).on('click', '#downloademail', function(){
	
	var attrbb = $(this).closest('.get-app-form').find('#getCntryFrm');
	var gettitleval=attrbb.attr('title');
	
	$('#dmpqph_ccode').val(gettitleval);
	
	if(gettitleval=="91" && gettitleval!='') {
		$('#downloademail').hide();
		$('#dispvalsme').html('mobile number');
		$('#sndtxt').html('Text me the link');
	}
	else {
		$('#downloademail').show();
		$('#dispvalsme').html('email id');
		$('#sndtxt').html('Send me the link');
	}
});

function ValidateEmail(demail) {
	if (/^\w+([\.-]?\w+)*@\w+([\.-]?\w+)*(\.\w{2,3})+$/.test(demail))  {
		return (true)
	}
    return (false)
}
	

function senddownloadlink() {
	
	$('#downloadmobile').removeClass('error');
	$('#downloademail').removeClass('error');
	
	var dmobile = $('#downloadmobile').val();
	var demail = $('#downloademail').val();
	var contcode = $('#dmpqph_ccode').val();
	
	if(contcode=='91' && dmobile=='' && (dmobile<10 || dmobile>10)) {
		$('#downloadmobile').addClass('error');
		return false;
	}
	else if(contcode!='91') {
		
		var vemail = ValidateEmail(demail);	
		if(demail=='' || vemail==false) {
			$('#downloademail').addClass('error');
			return false;
		}
	}
	
	$.ajax({
		type:'POST',
		url:loc_main+'/download-app.php',
		data:'frm=indexpage&action_enquiry=downloadapp&dmobile='+dmobile+'&demail='+demail,
		beforeSend: function () {
			//$('#submit').attr("disabled","disabled");
		},
		success:function(msg){
			if(msg == 'done'){
				alert("App Download Link Successfully Send");
				
				$('#downloadmobile').val('');
				$('#downloademail').val('');
			}
		}
	});
}
</script>

							<script>
								function pqreadCookie(name) {
									var nameEQ = name + "=";
									var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
									for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
										var c = ca[i];
										while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') c = c.substring(1, c.length);
										if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length, c.length);
									}
									return null;
								}

								function popCompFrm(compID, prodID = '', contView = '', whtsApp = '', inqVwFrm = '') {

									let isOlderThanOneDay = false;

									const createdTime = parseInt(pqreadCookie('otp_response_time') || 0);
									const mobileNo = pqreadCookie('mobileNo');
									const email = pqreadCookie('email');
                                     const city = pqreadCookie('city');
									if (createdTime) {
										const now = Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000);
										const diff = now - createdTime;

										if (diff >= 86400) { // 1 day = 86400 seconds
											isOlderThanOneDay = true;
										}
										// if (diff >= 1200) {   // 20 minutes
										// 		isOlderThanOneDay = true;
										// 	}

									}


									var verified_contact = pqreadCookie("verified_contact");
									var msg = pqreadCookie("otp_response");
									msg = decodeURIComponent(msg).replace(/\s/g, "");
									var msgval = msg.split("^");
									/* ---------- OTP FLOW START ---------- */

									if (verified_contact !== "V" && (msgval[0] === "send_otp_sms" || msgval[0] === "send_otp_email")) {
										var checkIcon = ` <svg width="12" height="11" viewBox="0 0 16 11" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M1 5.4L5.4 9.8L14.2 1" stroke="white" stroke-width="1.76" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"></path> </svg>`;
										$('.pbitem-box:nth-child(1) .pb-circle')
											.addClass('active completed')
											.html(checkIcon);
										$('.pbitem-box:nth-child(2) .pb-circle')
											.addClass('active completed')
											.html(checkIcon);
										$("#companyInquiry").show(); // Always use this container
										if (!msg) {
											console.warn("OTP cookie missing");
											return;
										}
										let ajaxData = {
											id: "popUp",
											inqfrm: "sendenq",
											inqid: msgval[1],
											pRID: msgval[2],
											inqVwFrm,
											
										};
										if (isOlderThanOneDay) {
											ajaxData.compID = compID;
											ajaxData.prodID = prodID;
											ajaxData.contView = contView;
											ajaxData.whtsApp = whtsApp;

										} else {
											console.log("Split values:", msgval);
											ajaxData.compID = msgval[1];
											ajaxData.prodID = msgval[2];
											ajaxData.contView = msgval[4];
											ajaxData.whtsApp = msgval[5];

										}
										if (msgval[0] === "send_otp_sms") {
											ajaxData.action = "smsOtpA";
											ajaxData.mobileNo = mobileNo || '';
											ajaxData.city = city;
											$.ajax({
												type: "POST",
												url: "https://www.dial4trade.com/popup_inquiry_v7.php",
												data: ajaxData,
												success: function(res) {
													$("#inqstep-1").html(res);
												}
											});
										}
										if (msgval[0] === "send_otp_email") {
											ajaxData.action = "smsOtpMail";
											ajaxData.email = email || '';
											ajaxData.city = city;
											$.ajax({
												type: "POST",
												url: "https://www.dial4trade.com/popup_inquiry_v7.php",
												data: ajaxData,
												success: function(res) {
													$("#inqstep-1").html(res);
												}
											});

										}

										return;
									}

									/* ---------- OTP FLOW END ---------- */
									//work for company inquiry popup
									var frmPopCompInqIDVal = $('#frmPopCompInqID').val();
									$('#compDePopDisp').show();
									if (prodID != '') {
										$.ajax({
											type: 'POST',
											url: 'https://www.dial4trade.com/popup_inquiry_v7.php',
											data: 'action=prodInq&compStepShow=productInq&popCompProductID=' + prodID + '&frmPopCompInqID=' + compID + '&frm=compInq&contView=' + contView + '&whtsApp=' + whtsApp + "&inqVwFrm=" + inqVwFrm+'&city=' + city,
											success: function(msg1) {
												$("#inqstep-1").html('');
												$("#inqstep-1").html(msg1);
											}
										});
									} else if (frmPopCompInqIDVal != '') {

										$.ajax({
											type: 'POST',
											url: 'https://www.dial4trade.com/popup_inquiry_v7.php',
											data: 'action=compInq&id=popUp&frmPopCompInqID=' + frmPopCompInqIDVal + '&contView=' + contView + '&whtsApp=' + whtsApp+'&city='+city,
											success: function(msg1) {
												$("#inqstep-1").html('');
												$("#inqstep-1").html(msg1);
											}
										});
									}
								}
								$(document).ready(function() {
									// ********** Order Unit **********
									$(document).on('change', '.OrderUnitSelect', function() {
										var val = this.value;

										if (val === 'other') {
											$(this).next('.OrderUnitInput-wrap').show();
											$('#popProdEnqType').val('');
										} else {
											$(this).next('.OrderUnitInput-wrap')
												.hide()
												.find('.OrderUnitInput').val('');
											$('#popProdEnqType').val(val);
										}

									});
									$(document).on('keyup', '.OrderUnitInput', function(e) {
										e.stopPropagation();

										var value = $(this).val().trim();

										$('#popProdEnqType').val(value);
										$('.unit-list li').hide();
										if (value !== '') {
											$('.unit-list span:contains("' + value + '")')
												.closest('li')
												.show();
										}
									});


									$.expr[":"].contains = $.expr.createPseudo(function(arg) {
										return function(elem) {
											return $(elem).text().toUpperCase().indexOf(arg.toUpperCase()) >= 0;
										};
									});

									$(document).on('click', 'body', function(e) {
										e.stopPropagation();
										$('.unit-list').hide();
									})
									$(document).on('click', '.OrderUnitInput', function(e) {
										e.stopPropagation();

										$(this).closest('.OrderUnitInput-wrap').next('.unit-list').show();
									});

									$(document).on('click', '.unit-list span', function(e) {
										e.stopPropagation();
										var unitvalue = $(this).text();
										$(this).closest('.unit-list').siblings('.OrderUnitInput-wrap').find('.OrderUnitInput').val(unitvalue);
										$('#popProdEnqType').val(unitvalue); // Set value to hidden field
										$(this).closest('.unit-list').hide();
									});
								});
							</script>
						</div>
					</div>

<script>
	function getCookie(name) {
		var nameEQ = name + "=";
		var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
		for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
			var c = ca[i];
			while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') c = c.substring(1, c.length);
			if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length, c.length);
		}
		return null;
		}

	function resolveCity() {
		let inputCity = $('#popProdEnqCity').val();
		let cookieCity = getCookie('city');
		return inputCity || cookieCity || '';
	}
</script>

<script>
	function chkcrt() {

		$.ajax({
			type: 'POST',
			url: loc_main + '/ajax323/othCart.php',
			data: 'action=dispCcnt',

			success: function(msg1) {
				$('#dhccnt').html(msg1);
			}
		});
	}

	$(document).ready(function() {
		chkcrt();

		const myInput = document.getElementById('pqmobile');
		myInput.onpaste = e => e.preventDefault();
	})


	$('body').on('click', '.cart-modal-btn', function() {
		$('.cart-modal').addClass('active');
		$('body').addClass('fade');

		$.ajax({
			type: 'POST',
			url: loc_main + '/ajax323/othCart.php',
			data: 'action=dispCartModl',

			success: function(msg1) {
				$('#cartModDisp').html(msg1);
			}
		});
	});

	$('body').on('click', '.cart-head .close', function() {
		$('.cart-modal').removeClass('active');
		$('body').removeClass('fade');
	});

	$(document).on('keydown', 'body', function(event) {
		if (event.key == "Escape") {
			$('.cart-modal').removeClass('active');
			$('body').removeClass('fade');
		}
	});
</script>

<script>
	function getCookie(name) {
    const cname = name + "=";
    const decodedCookie = decodeURIComponent(document.cookie);
    const ca = decodedCookie.split(';');
    for (let i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
        let c = ca[i].trim();
        if (c.indexOf(cname) === 0) {
            return c.substring(cname.length, c.length);
        }
    }
    return "";
}

/* ================= READ COOKIE & PREFILL IMAGE ENQUIRY ================= */

var memberName = pqreadCookie("memberName");
var companyName = pqreadCookie("compname");
var mobileNo = pqreadCookie("mobileNo");
var email = pqreadCookie("email");
var sessionID = pqreadCookie("sessionID");
var city = pqreadCookie("city");
var countryCodePhone = pqreadCookie("countryCodePhone");
var countryCode = pqreadCookie("countryCode");
var verified_contact = pqreadCookie("verified_contact");

if (sessionID != "" && sessionID != null) {

    /* ===== NAME ===== */
    if (memberName) {
        var resmemberName = decodeURIComponent(memberName.replace(/\+/g, " "));
        $("#imgProdEnqMemName").val(resmemberName);
    }

    /* ===== EMAIL ===== */
    if (email) {
        var resEmail = decodeURIComponent(email.replace(/\+/g, " "));
        $("#imgProdEnqEmail").val(resEmail);

        if (verified_contact === 'V') {
            $("#imgProdEnqEmail").prop("readonly", true);
            $("#imgProdEnqEmail").prop("disabled", true);
        }
    }

    /* ===== MOBILE ===== */
    if (mobileNo) {
        $("#imgProdEnqMobile").val(mobileNo);

        if (verified_contact === 'V') {
            $("#imgProdEnqMobile").prop("readonly", true);
            $("#imgProdEnqMobile").prop("disabled", true);

            // Disable flag dropdown
            $('.selected-flag').css({
                'pointer-events': 'none',
                'opacity': '0.6'
            });
        }
    }

    /* ===== COUNTRY CODE ===== */
    if (countryCodePhone) {
        $("#imgProdEnqPhCcode").val(countryCodePhone);
    }

    if (countryCode) {
        $("#imgProdEnqCsCcode").val(countryCode);

        $(".selected-flag .iti-flag").removeClass().addClass("iti-flag " + countryCode);

        $("#imgProdEnqMobile").attr("minlength", "5");
        $("#imgProdEnqMobile").attr("maxlength", "15");
    } else {
        if (countryCodePhone == "91") {
            $(".selected-flag .iti-flag").addClass("in");
        }
    }

    /* ===== CITY ===== */
    if (city) {
        var rescity = decodeURIComponent(city.replace(/\+/g, " "));
        $("#imgProdEnqCity").val(rescity);
    }
}






	function funcPopInqy(compNm, prodNm, prDisp, compAdd, memId, imgsd, prodID, moqs, compLink, memNm, proUrl, websUrl) {

		$('#imgProdEnqQnty').removeClass('error_bdr');
		$('#imgProdEnqType').removeClass('error_bdr');
		$('#imgProdEnqMemName').removeClass('error_bdr');
		$('#imgProdEnqMobile').removeClass('error_bdr');
		$('#imgProdEnqCity').removeClass('error_bdr');
		$('#imgProdEnqEmail').removeClass('error_bdr');


		$('#imgProdEnqQnty').val('');
		$('#imgProdEnqType').val('');

		if (compNm == '') {
			$('#dcom').hide();
			$('#dcn').html('');
		} else {
			$('#dcom').show();
			$('#dcn').html(compNm);
		}

		if (compAdd == '') {
			$('#dads').hide();
			$('#ads').html('');
		} else {
			$('#dads').show();
			$('#ads').html(compAdd);
		}

		if (prDisp == '') {
			$('#dpri').hide();
			$('#dpri').html('');
		} else {
			$('#dpri').show();
			$('#dpri').html(prDisp);
		}

		if (moqs == '') {
			$('#dmoq').hide();
			$('#dmoq').html('');
		} else {
			$('#dmoq').show();
			$('#dmoq').html(moqs);
		}

		if (memNm == '') {
			$('#dnm').hide();
			$('#mn').html('');
		} else {
			$('#dnm').show();
			$('#mn').html(memNm);
		}

		if (proUrl == '') {
			proUrl = '#';
		}

		var popEn = "I am Interested to buy " + prodNm + ". Please share the best price quotation.";

		$('#imgProdEnqDesc').val(popEn);
		$('#imgCompInqID').val(memId);
		$('#imgCompInqurl').val(compLink);
		$('#imgProductID').val(prodID);
		$('#dpns').html(prodNm);
		$('#imgCompNm').val(compNm);
		$('#imgProdNm').val(prodNm);
		$('#dprodN').attr('href', proUrl);
		$('#comanc').attr('href', compLink);
		$('#dweb').hide();
		

		if (imgsd.includes(',')) {

			var parts = imgsd.split(',');

			$('#mImgLi').empty(); // clear previous results
			var ct = 0;

			$.each(parts, function(index, value) {

				$('#scrollUp').show();
				$('#scrollDown').show();

				if (ct == 0) {
					console.log(value,'value');
					$('#mImgLi').append('<li><figure class="active"><img src="' + $.trim(value) + '" alt="image"></figure></li>');
					$('#dispStImg').attr('src', $.trim(value));
					$('#bgImgDisp').attr('style', "background-image: url('" + $.trim(value) + "'); background-repeat: no-repeat;");
				} else {
					$('#mImgLi').append('<li><figure><img src="' + $.trim(value) + '" alt="image"></figure></li>');
					// $('#dispStImg').attr('src', $.trim(value));
					// $('#bgImgDisp').attr('style', "background-image: url('" + $.trim(value) + "'); background-repeat: no-repeat;");
				}

				ct = ct + 1;
			});
		} else {
			$('#scrollUp').hide();
			$('#scrollDown').hide();

			$('#mImgLi').html('<li><figure class="active"><img src="' + imgsd + '" alt="Image"></figure></li>');
			$('#dispStImg').attr('src', imgsd);
			$('#bgImgDisp').attr('style', "background-image: url('" + imgsd + "'); background-repeat: no-repeat;");
		}
	}

	var step = 25;
	var scrolling = false;
	$("#scrollUp").bind("click", function(event) {
		event.preventDefault();
		$(".pz-thumb-list").animate({
			scrollTop: "-=" + step + "px"
		});
	}).bind("mouseover", function(event) {
		scrolling = true;
		scrollContent("up");
	}).bind("mouseout", function(event) {
		scrolling = false;
	});
	$("#scrollDown").bind("click", function(event) {
		event.preventDefault();
		$(".pz-thumb-list").animate({
			scrollTop: "+=" + step + "px"
		});
	}).bind("mouseover", function(event) {
		scrolling = true;
		scrollContent("down");
	}).bind("mouseout", function(event) {
		scrolling = false;
	});

	function scrollContent(direction) {
		var amount = (direction === "up" ? "-=1px" : "+=1px");
		$(".pz-thumb-list").animate({
			scrollTop: amount
		}, 1, function() {
			if (scrolling) {
				scrollContent(direction);
			}
		});
	}

	$('body').on('click', '.pz-thumb-list figure', function() {
		$('.pz-thumb-list figure').removeClass('active');
		$(this).addClass('active');
		var thumbSrc = $(this).find('img').attr('src');
		$('.zoomdiv img').attr('src', thumbSrc);
		$('.zoomdiv').css("background-image", "url(" + thumbSrc + ")");
	});

	function PrdZoom(e) {
		var zoomer = e.currentTarget;
		e.offsetX ? offsetX = e.offsetX : offsetX = e.touches[0].pageX
		e.offsetY ? offsetY = e.offsetY : offsetX = e.touches[0].pageX
		x = offsetX / zoomer.offsetWidth * 100
		y = offsetY / zoomer.offsetHeight * 100
		zoomer.style.backgroundPosition = x + '% ' + y + '%';
	}

	$(function() {

		});

	function generateProductSlider() {

		var sliderHTML = '<div class="mb2-slider">';

		$('#mImgLi li').each(function(index) {

			var imgSrc = $(this).find('img').attr('src');

			if (imgSrc) {

				sliderHTML +=
					'<div class="inq-slide fadeSlide" style="' +
					(index === 0 ? 'display:block;' : 'display:none;') + '">' +
					'<img src="' + imgSrc + '" loading="lazy">' +
					'</div>';
			}
		});

		sliderHTML += '</div>';

		$('#compLogDis').html(sliderHTML);
	}
</script>

	<script type="text/javascript">
		function pqreadCookie(name) {
			var nameEQ = name + "=";
			var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
			for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
				var c = ca[i];
				while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') c = c.substring(1, c.length);
				if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length, c.length);
			}
			return null;
		}
	</script>

		function isNumberKey(evt) {
			var charCode = (evt.which) ? evt.which : event.keyCode;
			if (charCode != 46) {
				if (charCode > 31 && (charCode < 48 || charCode > 57)) {
					return false;
				} else {
					return true;
				}
			}
		}

				if (1 == e) {

							var o = document.createElement("iframe");
							o.setAttribute("frameborder", "0"), o.setAttribute("allowfullscreen", ""), o.setAttribute("width", "100%"), o.setAttribute("height", "auto"), o.setAttribute("src", "https://www.youtube.com/embed/" + t[a].dataset.embed), t[a].innerHTML = "", t[a].appendChild(o)
						}
						e = !1
					}
				}
			});
		});

	function getCookiehead(cname) {
		var name = cname + "=";
		var decodedCookie = decodeURIComponent(document.cookie);
		var ca = decodedCookie.split(';');

		for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
			var c = ca[i];
			while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {
				c = c.substring(1);
			}
			if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {
				return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
			}
		}
		return "";
	}
	//headerlogincok
	var coovals = getCookiehead('sessionID');
	if (coovals != '') {
		$('.headerlogincok').html('My Account');
	}
	$('#companyInquiry').on('click', '.mb2-close', function() {
		var memberName = getCookiehead('memberName');
		var verified_contact = getCookiehead('verified_contact');
		console.log(verified_contact, 'testing9');
		if ($('#inqstep-5').is(':visible') || $('#inqstep-3').is(':visible') || $('#inqstep-4').is(':visible')) {
			$("#prdZoomInq").hide();
			$("#companyInquiry").hide();
			if (verified_contact === 'Y' || verified_contact === 'V') {
				$("#modal2-thanks").show();
			}
		}
	});
</script>
